title: "The circle"
date: "2018-05-01"

toc: true
categories: type-theory
---

In this entry, we want to show some equivalences
between the circle and other higher inductive types.

{% comment %}

{: . equation }

  $$\sum\,{\mathbb{S}^1}\,(\mathsf{rec}_{\mathbb{S}^1}\, \mathcal{U}\,  2\,
  (\mathsf{ua}(\mathsf{rec}_{2}2 1_{2} 0_{2}))) \simeq \mathbb{S}^1.$$

I gave a talk giving one solution using the flattening lemma:

- [**Direct link PDF**](https://github.com/jonaprieto/flattenlem/files/2045561/Jonathan-Prieto-Cubides-The-Flattening-Lemma.pdf)

{% endcomment %}

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="616" class="Keyword">open</a> <a id="621" class="Keyword">import</a> <a id="628" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}" class="Module">2018-07-06-mini-hott</a>{% endraw %}</pre>

##  S¹ type

The circle is the higher inductive type with one point
and one no trivial path called path as we show in the following
picture.

![path](/assets/ipe-images/circle.png)
*Figure 1. The circle type `S¹`.*

## `pS` type

![path](/assets/ipe-images/tour-type.png)
*Figure 2. `pS` Type.*

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="1968" class="Keyword">private</a>

## Equivalences

### Lemma 1

{: .equation }

  $$ \mathsf{S}^{1} \simeq \mathsf{pS}. $$

**Proof**.

Let us define the outgoing functions:

The proof of the homotopy $$ f' ∘ g' \sim \mathsf{id}$$.

The proof of the homotopy $$g' ∘ f' \sim \mathsf{id}$$:

<pre class="Agda">{% raw %}<a id="8397" class="Comment">-- Homotopy</a>
  <a id="H₂"></a><a id="8411" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#8411" class="Function">H₂</a> <a id="8414" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8416" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#4142" class="Function">g&#39;</a> <a id="8419" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4719" class="Function Operator">∘</a> <a id="8421" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#4037" class="Function">f&#39;</a> <a id="8424" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#22398" class="Function Operator">∼</a> <a id="8426" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#4218" class="Function">id</a>
  <a id="8431" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#8411" class="Function">H₂</a> <a id="8434" class="Symbol">=</a> <a id="8436" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#1469" class="Function">S¹-ind</a> <a id="8443" class="Symbol">_</a> <a id="8445" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="8446" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6281" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8451" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#927" class="InductiveConstructor">!base</a><a id="8456" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="8458" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#8476" class="Function">q</a>
    <a id="8464" class="Keyword">where</a>
      <a id="8476" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#8476" class="Function">q</a> <a id="8478" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="8480" href="{% _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#927" class="InductiveConstructor">!base</a> <a id="8491" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14110" class="Function">==</a> <a id="8494" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#6281" class="Function">refl</a> <a id="8499" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md %}{% raw %}#927" class="InductiveConstructor">!base</a> <a id="8505" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-07-06-mini-hott.md %}{% raw %}#14110" class="Function">[</a> <a id="8507" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="8510" href="{% endraw %}{{ site.baseurl }}{% link _posts/2018-05-01-circle-puzzle.md ### Lemma 3

{: .equation}
  $$
    \Sigma~S^{1}~P~\simeq~pS
  $$

  where $$P (\mathsf{base}) :≡ \mathsf{Bool}$$ and $$\mathsf{ap~P~loop~=~ua~(neg)}$$.

    <a id="14550" class="Comment">-- p₁₀ ↦ (base, 1) == (base, 0)</a>
